## Idea

A type is `œÄ_n`-finite if it has finitely many connected components and all of its homotopy groups up to level `n` at all base points are finite.

<pre class="Agda">
<a id="6719" class="Comment">-- Section 1. œÄ-Finiteness</a>

<a id="6747" class="Comment">-- Definition 1.3</a>

<a id="6766" class="Comment">-- We introduce locally finite types</a>

<a id="is-locally-finite-Prop"></a><a id="6804" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6804" class="Function">is-locally-finite-Prop</a> <a id="6827" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="6831" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6832" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6832" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="6834" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6836" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="6841" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6843" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6845" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="6848" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6832" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="6850" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6852" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#1380" class="Function">UU-Prop</a> <a id="6860" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6832" class="Bound">l</a>
<a id="6862" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6804" class="Function">is-locally-finite-Prop</a> <a id="6885" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6885" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6887" class="Symbol">=</a>
